Forsvarets spesielle kommandosituasjonsrapport - Norwegian Special Forces Situation Report

----------------------------------------------

Objectives
1. Bring friendly civilian VIP to nuclear munitions.
2. Provide security while the VIP renders nuclear ordinance inert and safe.
3. Exfiltrate via SDV.

N.B. The Norwegian government cannot be seen to have been involved.
Tie up all loose ends.

----------------------------------------------

Signal
Commanding Element: 	TACCOM
Ranking Field Element: 	Hunter 6
1st Squad: 				Hunter 1-1
2nd Squad: 				Hunter 1-2
3rd Squad: 				Hunter 1-3
Hostile Anti-Air Radar:	Mike-26

----------------------------------------------

Intelligence
Satellite feed has been unable to locate the precise location of the objective warheads. We tracked the aircraft transporting the warheads from mainland North Korea, but lost track of it over the ocean due to cloud cover.
We have been monitoring Stratis' main airport, and the helo didn't land there. 

The missile system is believed to be at Mike-26, however, it is unknown if the warheads are there yet.

The enemy can bring vastly superior firepower to muster. It would be advisable to delay alerting their headquarters on Stratis to our presence for as long as possible.
Their guards change shift every 8 hours. The next change of shift should be at 1930. That means we have until 0330 hours the guards are expected to be elsewhere, and new men come in.

Satelite feed has confirmed at least one flight of gunship helicopters at the airfield.
We have no intelligence on possible armoured threats, however a few armed troop transports have shown up on satellite.
Naval Patrols are moderate.

The island is mostly occupied by military forces, with a minor civilian presence that is fiercely loyal to our foe.

Forecast is currently partly overcast, 35% POPs overnight, clearing up by dawn.

----------------------------------------------

Journal Entry
18:19
Thursday, September 14th, 2017

Our Norwegian government negotiated for and received increased US military presence to buffer Russian aggression. This has halted Russian belligerence in Scandinavia, however, having friends is a two-way street. 
The Americans are asking for our help in a covert operation. Escalation of rhetoric between America and North Korea have boiled over. The Americans have decided to take action.

Of course, they couldn't be seen to be responsible if the operation goes pear shaped. That's where we come in. Their navy has provided transport for us. Perhaps we might be able to ask for more support, as long as they're not seen to be involved. They do have navy fire support and carriers in the area...
Not that we want the world to know Norway is conducting black ops on another sovereign nation's soil...
Due to the highly sensitive nature of this operation, no friendlies are to be captured alive. Further, you will be either exfiltrating with friendly KIAs, or ensuring that they are untraceable.

We are tasked with infiltrating the most remote North Korean nuclear missile system. 
Due to the volatile nature of nuclear ordinance, we have brought along a VIP: Dr. Fabio Gianotti. His responsibility is to render the nuclear muitions inoperable and safe.
Any attempt to destroy or otherwise tamper with nuclear munitions is strictly prohibited. Leave the science to him.

We have infiltrated via SDV yesterday, and are preparing to make tracks. We'll wait for nightfall.

----------------------------------------------

Restrictions/Recommendations
No Blufor tracking
No drawing on map after you leave the starting point. You can map gesture if you need to.
At most 8 + 1 mags for primary
At most 8 grenades in total
Suppressors recommended
HK 416 or the like (https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_equipment_of_the_Norwegian_Army)

1 Reinforcement wave, at either TACCOM's or Hunter 6's discretion may be called in via SDV appropriate secured harbour or coastline. //TODO
No asset respawns

Time acceleration will be on approximately 5 - 10x.
Hunter 6 is able to request time skip.

With Hunter 6's prior approval, you may commandeer any enemy asset. We need all the help we can get.

-------------------------------------------------
